	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml') !== '6bfbf32a784820a54c84c4512e6cbf86335b9265') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml') !== '2a565afbb8e9937128ba68cbdedbcb2e5aabb150') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml') !== '6bfbf32a784820a54c84c4512e6cbf86335b9265') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/codeStyles/codeStyleConfig.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') != '9fd7be707c7183a15b15554b95dd7137aed32d2e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '9fd7be707c7183a15b15554b95dd7137aed32d2e') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '7e01767f8dd0f2bb4ff93bd23364bbd8836f371f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '9fd7be707c7183a15b15554b95dd7137aed32d2e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('.idea/php.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/php.xml');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('.idea/php.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/php.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') != '36609362f317573125074570a12ec42881b8245b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/php.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/php.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/php.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== '36609362f317573125074570a12ec42881b8245b') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== 'bbf68a424e9bf71daef1e150f5fefc68ad91ca17') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/php.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/php.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/php.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/php.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== '36609362f317573125074570a12ec42881b8245b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/php.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/workspace.xml');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') != '121f1338dfb9cd83596f3e9e5bf85cddefa44b24') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/workspace.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/workspace.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '121f1338dfb9cd83596f3e9e5bf85cddefa44b24') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'd29d88e64c6f870ec2aed85343a1ec48691f33c5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/workspace.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/workspace.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/workspace.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/workspace.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '121f1338dfb9cd83596f3e9e5bf85cddefa44b24') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != 'abf1c43b0075d03936c7e4a2d4fb891c2f22b8ac') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'abf1c43b0075d03936c7e4a2d4fb891c2f22b8ac') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '13d0fc32d84a51e6a928f63f0a8d9a30fb25843e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'abf1c43b0075d03936c7e4a2d4fb891c2f22b8ac') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '4339a67f82539f11f9c8cabd4882beb3deadc121') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '4339a67f82539f11f9c8cabd4882beb3deadc121') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '32355ac4d3ab110f0cb8c3292612a45bd38b6b94') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '4339a67f82539f11f9c8cabd4882beb3deadc121') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') != 'f17ed1bb6256e6ce9a8752af23cba7a60c83cb39') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== 'f17ed1bb6256e6ce9a8752af23cba7a60c83cb39') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== '35e11e218a607914ed279b34e09bb0a4f93fc136') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== 'f17ed1bb6256e6ce9a8752af23cba7a60c83cb39') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.css.php');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') != '9f9ce59cf569cdbaf80453dac2163253a20524ee') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '9f9ce59cf569cdbaf80453dac2163253a20524ee') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '59803125b9939ad73cc33d9e5565ae7372cc8c67') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '9f9ce59cf569cdbaf80453dac2163253a20524ee') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}
